This renderer is supported on all \doxylink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal}{Universal} RP supported platforms. struct \mbox{\hyperlink{struct_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_1_1_rendering_data}{Rendering\+Data}}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Struct that flattens several rendering settings used to render a camera stack. URP builds the {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_1_1_rendering_data}{Rendering\+Data}} settings from several places, including the pipeline asset, camera and light settings. The settings also might vary on different platforms and depending on if Adaptive Performance is used. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item

\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Holds information about the post-\/processing anti-\/aliasing mode. When set to {\ttfamily None} no post-\/processing anti-\/aliasing pass will be performed. When set to {\ttfamily Fast} a fast approximated anti-\/aliasing pass will render when resolving the camera to screen. When set to {\ttfamily Subpixel\+Morphological\+Anti\+Aliasing} SMAA pass will render when resolving the camera to screen. You can choose the SMAA quality by setting \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
Antialiasing\+Quality


\end{DoxySeeAlso}
. \end{DoxyCompactList}\item 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5}{Camera\+Render\+Type}} \{ \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5a095a1b43effec73955e31e790438de49}{Base}}

 \}
\begin{DoxyCompactList}\small\item\em Holds information about the render type of a camera. Options are Base or Overlay. Base rendering type allows the camera to render to either the screen or to a texture. \doxysubsection{Enumeration Type Documentation}
\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_aaf8cbc8e354ffbf881fca37559bb0b1d}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!AntialiasingMode@{AntialiasingMode}}
\index{AntialiasingMode@{AntialiasingMode}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{AntialiasingMode}{AntialiasingMode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_aaf8cbc8e354ffbf881fca37559bb0b1d} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_aaf8cbc8e354ffbf881fca37559bb0b1d}{Unity\+Engine.\+Rendering.\+Universal.\+Antialiasing\+Mode}}}



Holds information about the post-\/processing anti-\/aliasing mode. When set to {\ttfamily None} no post-\/processing anti-\/aliasing pass will be performed. When set to {\ttfamily Fast} a fast approximated anti-\/aliasing pass will render when resolving the camera to screen. When set to {\ttfamily Subpixel\+Morphological\+Anti\+Aliasing} SMAA pass will render when resolving the camera to screen. You can choose the SMAA quality by setting \begin{DoxySeeAlso}{See also}
\doxylink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a6a05a462f042ca935690a27bb92f3dfa}{Antialiasing\+Quality}


\end{DoxySeeAlso}
.

\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!CameraOverrideOption@{CameraOverrideOption}}
\index{CameraOverrideOption@{CameraOverrideOption}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CameraOverrideOption}{CameraOverrideOption}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb}{Unity\+Engine.\+Rendering.\+Universal.\+Camera\+Override\+Option}}}



Holds information about whether to override certain camera rendering options from the render pipeline asset. When set to {\ttfamily Off} option will be disabled regardless of what is set on the pipeline asset. When set to {\ttfamily On} option will be enabled regardless of what is set on the pipeline asset. When set to {\ttfamily Use\+Pipeline\+Setting} value set in the \doxylink{class_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_1_1_universal_render_pipeline_asset}{Universal\+Render\+Pipeline\+Asset}. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Off@{Off}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Off@{Off}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bbad15305d7a4e34e02489c74a5ef542f36}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb} 
Off&Use this to disable regardless of what is set on the pipeline asset. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{On@{On}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!On@{On}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bba521c36a31c2762741cf0f8890cbe05e3}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb} 
On&Use this to enable regardless of what is set on the pipeline asset. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{UsePipelineSettings@{UsePipelineSettings}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!UsePipelineSettings@{UsePipelineSettings}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bba79f75f7c3f6f5165c7a9b7a10c8c7601}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a8222916e4c4c8322f82ca8b14ad756bb} 
Use\+Pipeline\+Settings&Use this to choose the setting set on the pipeline asset. \\

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

\index{CameraRenderType@{CameraRenderType}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{CameraRenderType}{CameraRenderType}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5}{Unity\+Engine.\+Rendering.\+Universal.\+Camera\+Render\+Type}}}



Holds information about the render type of a camera. Options are Base or Overlay. Base rendering type allows the camera to render to either the screen or to a texture. Overlay rendering type allows the camera to render on top of a previous camera output, thus compositing camera results. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Base@{Base}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Base@{Base}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5a095a1b43effec73955e31e790438de49}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5} 
Base&Use this to select the base camera render type. Base rendering type allows the camera to render to either the screen or to a texture. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Overlay@{Overlay}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Overlay@{Overlay}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5a6b551379c3c0b59326abdaf3b4395bd3}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af54eede616e112c00931fdfeb92a87e5} 
Overlay&Use this to select the overlay camera render type. Overlay rendering type allows the camera to render on top of a previous camera output, thus compositing camera results. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

Forward\+Plus&Render all objects and lighting in one pass using a clustered data structure to access lighting data. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Deferred@{Deferred}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Deferred@{Deferred}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ab2b1b5c68947b640d3fd9c64170e6419a4ed71db54748b36eeb398876b0c747ac}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ab2b1b5c68947b640d3fd9c64170e6419} 
Deferred&Render all objects first in a g-\/buffer pass, then apply all lighting in a separate pass using deferred shading. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}

Before\+Rendering&Executes a {\ttfamily \doxylink{class_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_1_1_scriptable_render_pass}{Scriptable\+Render\+Pass}} before rendering any other passes in the pipeline. Camera matrices and stereo rendering are not setup this point. You can use this to draw to custom input textures used later in the pipeline, f.\+ex LUT textures. \\

\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{StoreActionsOptimization}{StoreActionsOptimization}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65}{Unity\+Engine.\+Rendering.\+Universal.\+Store\+Actions\+Optimization}}}



Defines if \doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} discards or stores the render targets of the Draw\+Objects Passes. Selecting the Store option significantly increases the memory bandwidth on mobile and tile-\/based GPUs. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Auto@{Auto}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Auto@{Auto}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65a06b9281e396db002010bde1de57262eb}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65} 
Auto&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} uses the Discard option by default, and falls back to the Store option if it detects any injected Passes. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Discard@{Discard}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Discard@{Discard}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65ad94b42030b9785fd754d5c1754961269}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65} 
Discard&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} discards the render targets of render Passes that are not reused later (lower memory bandwidth). \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Store@{Store}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Store@{Store}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65afdb0c388de01d545017cdf9ccf00eb72}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_a3b397e122ca0ac288bcc2e027eb9da65} 
Store&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} stores all render targets of each Pass (higher memory bandwidth). \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!TonemappingMode@{TonemappingMode}}
\index{TonemappingMode@{TonemappingMode}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{TonemappingMode}{TonemappingMode}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464} 
enum \mbox{\hyperlink{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464}{Unity\+Engine.\+Rendering.\+Universal.\+Tonemapping\+Mode}}}



Options to select a tonemapping algorithm to use for color grading. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{None@{None}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!None@{None}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464a6adf97f83acf6453d4a6a4b1070f3754}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464} 
None&Use this option if you do not want to apply tonemapping. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Neutral@{Neutral}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Neutral@{Neutral}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464ae9bb5320b3890b6747c91b5a71ae5a01}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464} 
Neutral&Use this option if you only want range-\/remapping with minimal impact on color hue and saturation. It is generally a great starting point for extensive color grading. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{ACES@{ACES}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!ACES@{ACES}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464a01ec90d9624dce53f3f3492882841fe6}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_ae8d269006cefbb42eaf2081c4fce5464} 
ACES&Use this option to apply a close approximation of the reference ACES tonemapper for a more filmic look. It is more contrasted than Neutral and has an effect on actual color hue and saturation. Note that if you use this tonemapper all the grading operations will be done in the ACES color spaces for optimal precision and results. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!UpscalingFilterSelection@{UpscalingFilterSelection}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2}

Defines the upscaling filter selected by the user the universal render pipeline asset. 

\begin{DoxyEnumFields}{Enumerator}
\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Auto@{Auto}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Auto@{Auto}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2a06b9281e396db002010bde1de57262eb}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2} 
Auto&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} selects a filtering option automatically based on the Render Scale value and the current screen resolution. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Linear@{Linear}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Linear@{Linear}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2a32a843da6ea40ab3b17a3421ccdf671b}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2} 
Linear&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} uses Bilinear filtering to perform upscaling. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{Point@{Point}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!Point@{Point}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2a2a3cd5946cfd317eb99c3d32e35e2d4c}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2} 
Point&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} uses Nearest-\/\+Neighbour filtering to perform upscaling. \\
\hline

\raisebox{\heightof{T}}[0pt][0pt]{\index{FSR@{FSR}!UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}}\index{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal@{UnityEngine.Rendering.Universal}!FSR@{FSR}}}\Hypertarget{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2aa8847ff460e700f63a54f06a667534b1}\label{namespace_unity_engine_1_1_rendering_1_1_universal_af539fda77acea2b3d4b611576bbb47d2} 
FSR&\doxylink{namespace_unity}{Unity} uses the AMD FSR 1.\+0 technique to perform upscaling. \\
\hline

\end{DoxyEnumFields}
